Startable/Stoppable service lifecycle pattern through a trait-based interface and coordinated shutdown sequence. The core architecture is as follows:\\n\\n## Core Lifecycle Interface\\n\\nThe `Server` trait defined in `core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/Server.scala` is the primary lifecycle interface, defining three core methods: `startup()`, `shutdown()`, and `awaitShutdown()`. This trait serves as the contract for all major server components.\\n\\n## Service Hierarchy and Startup Ordering\\n\\n**KafkaRaftServer** (`core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/KafkaRaftServer.scala`) is the top-level orchestrator that manages both broker and controller server lifecycles. Its startup follows a dependency-aware order:\\n1. Controller starts first (via `controller.foreach(_.startup())`)\\n2. Broker starts second (via `broker.foreach(_.startup())`)\\n\\nThis ordering ensures that the broker can depend on controller availability for registration and coordination.\\n\\n## BrokerServer Shutdown Pattern\\n\\n**BrokerServer** (`core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/BrokerServer.scala`) implements a carefully orchestrated LIFO (Last In, First Out) shutdown sequence that ensures dependent services stop in reverse order. The shutdown orchestration (lines 729-843) follows this sequence:\\n\\n1. Controlled shutdown notification to controller\\n2. Socket server request processing halt\\n3. Request processor pool shutdown\\n4. KafkaApis handler closure\\n5. Scheduler shutdown (critical early shutdown)\\n6. Transaction and group coordinator shutdown\\n7. Replica Manager shutdown (with replica fetcher threads and purgatory)\\n8. Alter Partition Manager shutdown\\n9. Channel managers closure\\n10. Log Manager shutdown with state persistence\\n11. Remote log manager graceful closure\\n12. Quota managers shutdown\\n13. Socket server final shutdown\\n14. Lifecycle manager signal\\n\\nThis sequence ensures that services dependent on scheduler functionality are shut down before the scheduler, and all request handling is halted before closing underlying network and storage components.\\n\\n## ControllerServer Shutdown Pattern\\n\\n**ControllerServer** (`core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/ControllerServer.scala`) follows a similar pattern:\\n1. transitions through `compareAndSet()` operations to manage state changes: SHUTDOWN → STARTING → STARTED → SHUTTING_DOWN, preventing concurrent startup/shutdown and ensuring idempotent Request processor pool shutdown\\n4. KafkaApis handler closure\\n5. Scheduler shutdown (critical early shutdown)\\n6. Transaction and group coordinator shutdown\\n7.
